Based on risk knowledge and the role First Air takes in preventing contamination ingress into the Grade A zone, operators need to position themselves so protective airflow passes over body parts inserted into the RABS (such as hands and sleeves) and into the surrounding cleanroom. Positioning of materials ready for transfer should also consider protective airflow exiting the RABS Grade A zone and from the overhead or over-open-door UDAF. AVS should demonstrate the appropriate airflow from the interior of the RABS to the surrounding area.

Materials and parts should be presented for transfer at working position, typically on carts.

A secondary operator could support positioning parts and materials provided they do not compromise the protective airflow.

Good aseptic technique (e.g., transfer of inner bag at the RABS interface by double-bag methods) is required on open-barrier-door entry, and the operator's reach should be limited to the required task without touching other surfaces, critical or otherwise. Practices of hand disinfection prior to open-door interventions should be based on the contact time recommended and qualified practices. (See PDA TR-62 for additional information.)

During the intervention, EM sampling locations in the proximity of the intervention should be subject to continuous EM (i.e., viable and nonviable). The surrounding cleanroom should also be monitored at the door opening/operator interface. (See Topic 5.)

Installation of sterilized RABS gloves after open-door setup is commonly done as the final procedure. (See Topic 9.)

Before and at the time barrier doors are closed, the inside of the barrier door should be disinfected. The RABS gloves should be drawn back so only the RABS glove port entry interface should require disinfection (in some cases, covers may be inserted to prevent RABS glove contamination at open-door interventions).

With the barrier door closed, full EM should be implemented and should be ready for monitoring throughout the production-readiness setup.

Installation setup of all critical parts requires good aseptic technique, possibly with the use of tools (e.g., tweezers, tongs) and throughout the procedure. First Air protection should not be compromised.

Rationale

As interventions are such a high-risk activity, best practice is needed in all cases to mitigate risks to an acceptable level.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Two Setup Conditions (兩階段 Setup)：RABS 的 setup 分為兩個截然不同的階段，風險等級完全不同：

First Air (第一氣流)：指從 HEPA 過濾器出來後，尚未接觸任何物體或人員的潔淨氣流。在 open-door setup 時，操作員必須確保 First Air 從 RABS 內部流向外部，經過操作員的手和袖子後排出。這是防止外部污染進入 Grade A 區域的第一道防線。

Double-Bag Method (雙袋法)：將滅菌物品的外層包裝在 RABS 介面處移除，僅將內層（無菌）包裝傳入 Grade A 區域的技術。這是維持無菌傳遞的標準做法。

比喻說明 Analogy

RABS 的 setup 就像手術室的術前準備：

  • Phase 1 (門開啟) = 將滅菌器械從運送車搬入手術室。此時手術室門開著，風險最高，必須快速且有紀律地完成。護理人員的位置不能阻擋層流氣流。
  • Phase 2 (門關閉) = 手術室門關閉後，進行器械的精細擺放與最終確認。此時環境受控，但仍需穿戴無菌手套操作。
  • First Air = 就像手術室天花板的層流罩，潔淨空氣必須從上方往下流過器械台，再向外排出，操作人員不能站在氣流的「上游」。

重點提示 Key Notes

Open-Door Setup 的最佳實務檢查清單：

  1. 操作員定位 -- 保護性氣流經過手/袖後流向潔淨室（不可阻擋 First Air）
  2. 物料擺放 -- 待傳遞物料放在工作高度的推車上
  3. 副操作員 -- 可協助定位，但不得影響保護性氣流
  4. 無菌技術 -- 使用雙袋法傳遞；操作範圍限於必要任務
  5. 手部消毒 -- 開門介入前，依合格程序進行手部消毒（參考 PDA TR-62）
  6. 持續 EM -- 介入期間鄰近位置持續進行環境監控（viable + nonviable）
  7. 手套安裝 -- 開門 setup 的最後步驟才安裝滅菌 RABS 手套
  8. 門內側消毒 -- 關門前/關門時對門內側進行消毒

設計原則 Design Principle

原文強調：「As much as possible, set-up should be performed with the doors closed」。這意味著 RABS 的設備設計應盡量讓操作人員能透過手套口或 RTP 完成大部分 setup 工作，將必須開門的操作降到最低。這是設備採購規格（URS）中應明確要求的設計理念。

對 CDMO 而言，選購 RABS 設備時，應評估「多少 setup 操作可在關門狀態下完成」作為重要的設備評選標準。能在關門狀態下完成更多 setup 的設備，代表更低的污染風險和更高的無菌保證水準。

實務應用 Practical Application

你正在為一條新的 RABS 充填線撰寫 Setup SOP，以下是需要定義的關鍵項目：

  • 開門操作清單：列出所有必須在開門狀態下完成的操作，並為每一項定義最大允許時間
  • 操作員站位圖：標示主操作員與副操作員的位置，確保不阻擋保護性氣流方向
  • EM 取樣點：在開門介入區域周邊設置連續監控點
  • 關門檢查表：門內側消毒完成、手套安裝確認、完整 EM 啟動
  • AVS 結果參考：附上 AVS 確效報告中的氣流方向示意圖，作為操作員訓練教材

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 RABS 手套的安裝是 open-door setup 的「最後步驟」？如果先安裝手套再傳入其他物料，會有什麼問題？
  2. 原文提到 AVS 應展示「RABS 內部到周圍區域的適當氣流」。在 open-door setup 時，理想的氣流方向應該是什麼？為什麼？
  3. 如果你是設備供應商，你會如何設計 RABS 來最大化「關門狀態下可完成的 setup 操作」比例？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • APS 先決條件：潔淨室確效、RABS 確效（HEPA/壓差/AVS）、人員訓練、介入清單、物料傳遞方法、EM 計畫 -- 六項缺一不可
  • 事件驅動原則：污染是「事件」的結果而非「時間」的結果 -- APS 時長不需等於最長生產時間，關鍵是模擬所有可能引入污染的事件
  • Worst-Case 邊界：最差條件必須在合理操作範圍內；APS 不能用來驗證不良設計或操作實務
  • RABS 獨特優勢：因物理屏障的存在，hold time、充填時長、人員數量、充填速度等傳統 worst-case 參數對 RABS 的影響較低
  • Open-Door 最高風險：open-door intervention（包含 setup）是 RABS 中風險最高的操作，應是 APS worst-case 設計的焦點
  • 兩階段 Setup：開門階段（最高風險）與關門階段（受控環境）的操作要求截然不同，設備設計應盡量讓 setup 在關門狀態下完成
  • Piggyback APS 的限制：可作為整體 APS 方案的補充，但不能單獨使用，因為它無法模擬 setup 階段
9

Topic 9: Best Practices & References

最佳實務與參考 | p95-p115

PDA Points to Consider No. 12 (2025) — RABS | p95 - p115

本章學習目標

  • 理解 RABS 中 closed-door 與 open-door intervention 均須遵循無菌操作技術的原因與風險差異
  • 掌握 intervention 的資格確認（qualification）流程，包括風險評估、AVS 文件化與 APS 納入
  • 學習 First Air 原則在介入操作設計中的關鍵角色及其受限時的緩解措施
  • 了解 RABS 手套不得接觸 critical surfaces 的規範，以及接觸後應採取的措施
  • 認識 open-door intervention 後所需之額外控制措施（消毒、棄置、取樣、EM 監控等）
  • 熟悉 intervention 執行的標準化流程：清線、手套穿戴、視覺檢查、無菌工具使用
  • 掌握 RABS 手套安裝的三種業界方法及其各自的優勢與風險考量
  • 理解 RABS 手套在操作期間的消毒策略與殺孢子劑使用時機

Q 9.1 Aseptic Techniques for Closed- and Open-Door Interventions

原文內容 Original Text

Q 9.1. Is it necessary to use the same aseptic techniques and practices when performing closed- and open-door interventions in the restricted access barrier system (RABS)?

Recommendation

To ensure product sterility, operators performing aseptic operations must adhere to aseptic techniques for both closed- and open-door interventions. As part of a company's comprehensive CCS, a risk assessment must be developed to ensure all intervention steps are appropriately defined, including required mitigation actions, for qualified interventions. All open-door interventions are to be minimized and should have a qualified maximum time limit.

When assessing the risk of an intervention, the following should be considered:

  • Overall contamination risk to product (e.g., open units, exposed components), based on personnel location, movement, and/or RABS glove proximity
  • Maintenance of First Air
  • Including the accessibility of the area to perform the intervention
  • Supported with AVS
  • Consideration of line clearance (e.g., removal of compromised units)
  • Disinfection
  • Area where the intervention takes place needs to be accessible for disinfection, if required (Disinfection prior to EM should be avoided.)
  • Monitoring the intervention
  • Viable (e.g., surface(s), operator(s),) and total particulates
  • Start and end time of intervention (i.e., duration)
  • Before resuming operation, appropriate evaluation and line clearances performed (e.g., disinfection, verified removal of compromised units)

Note: See Topic 4 for clarification on recommended aseptic techniques.

Furthermore, while a RABS with closed doors provides an improved separation between the operator and the product, it decreases the likelihood of nonsterile product; therefore, the risk is still present and should be appropriately controlled.

Rationale

While a RABS with closed doors provides enhanced protection of the product between the operator and extraneous contamination sources (e.g., operator, environment), proper aseptic technique is still required to aid in the overall control of the product. A risk assessment should be documented outlining the necessary controls required to maintain product sterility.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Closed-door vs. Open-door Intervention (關門介入 vs. 開門介入)：在 RABS 中，即使門是關閉的，操作人員透過手套進行的介入仍然存在污染風險。PDA 的立場非常明確：不論門是開或關，都必須遵循相同的無菌操作技術。

Qualified Maximum Time Limit (經過資格確認的最長時限)：所有 open-door intervention 都必須設定經過驗證的最長允許時間。這不是隨意訂定的數字，而是透過風險評估、AVS 和 EM 數據所支持的。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像手術室中的無菌操作：即使外科醫師戴著手套（類似 closed-door），他仍必須遵循嚴格的無菌技術，不能因為「有手套保護」就放鬆警覺。而當需要打開器械包（類似 open-door intervention）時，風險更高，所需的控制措施也更多。RABS 的邏輯完全相同 -- 屏障降低風險，但不消除風險。

重點提示 Key Notes

EU Annex 1 對齊：此建議直接呼應 EU Annex 1 的核心精神 -- CCS 必須涵蓋所有介入操作。文件中特別強調「Disinfection prior to EM should be avoided」，這是因為如果在 EM 取樣前就先消毒，你就無法真正評估介入操作帶來的污染風險。

時間記錄的重要性：每次介入必須記錄開始與結束時間。這不僅是 GDocP 要求，更是事後調查異常時的關鍵數據來源。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 PDA 建議在 EM 取樣之前不應先進行消毒？如果先消毒了，對數據解讀會有什麼影響？
  2. 貴公司目前的 CCS 是否有涵蓋 closed-door intervention 的風險評估？如果沒有，可能有什麼法規風險？
  3. 如何設計一個系統來自動記錄 intervention 的持續時間，而不依賴人工記錄？
Q 9.2 Qualification and Approval of Interventions

原文內容 Original Text

Q 9.2. How should interventions be qualified and approved for use in routine production?

Recommendation

All interventions should be included in a documented risk assessment associated with a comprehensive CCS. This documented risk assessment should consider the following risk factors:

  • Duration of the intervention (in minutes)
  • Complexity of the intervention (number of steps)
  • Proximity of the intervention to sterile components (equipment, product)
  • Exposure of personnel

Additional factors may be considered when assessing the risk associated with execution of an intervention. The assessment must consider the use of sterile equipment and tools (e.g., forceps) to minimize impact on the RABS environment when performing an intervention.

All qualified interventions should have the airflow visualization recorded and documented to ensure that the impact of performing the interventions are thoroughly understood. This includes inherent and corrective interventions that can be performed through RABS gloves and open-door activities. First Air principles shall be included in this airflow visualization and must not be ignored during execution of interventions. Based on mechanical or physical limitations, if proper First Air principles cannot be followed, it must be documented within the risk assessment, and proper mitigations (e.g., material discard) must be established. It is recommended that, as much as possible, mitigations be automated, ensuring proper execution each time the intervention is performed. The inclusion of qualified interventions to be performed during routine production should be included in the firm's APS program.

Rationale

Following the process recommended above would ensure the inclusion of QRM principles through a documented risk assessment to be included in a comprehensive CCS. The proper design, followed by risk analysis and airflow visualization, will provide the appropriate understanding of the intervention to approve its use, during routine production, and for execution in a firm's APS program. The execution of interventions, to be performed during routine production, are to be included in a firm's APS program.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Intervention Qualification (介入操作資格確認)：每一個 intervention 在被允許用於日常生產前，都必須經過完整的資格確認流程。PDA 提出了四大風險因子：

  • 持續時間 (Duration)：越長風險越高
  • 複雜度 (Complexity)：步驟越多，出錯機率越高
  • 接近度 (Proximity)：離無菌組件越近，污染風險越大
  • 人員暴露 (Exposure)：操作人員介入的程度

AVS (Airflow Visualization Study，氣流可視化研究)：所有 qualified intervention 都必須有 AVS 記錄。這不是「做過一次就好」，而是要確保每個 intervention 對 First Air 的影響都被充分理解並文件化。

比喻說明 Analogy

把 intervention qualification 想成飛行員的飛行前檢查清單 (preflight checklist)。飛行員不會因為「飛過很多次」就跳過檢查。同樣地，每個 intervention 都需要一份完整的「飛行計畫」：你要知道會經過哪些風險區域（proximity）、需要多長時間（duration）、有多少步驟（complexity），以及誰會參與（exposure）。只有通過這些審查的 intervention 才能被「核可起飛」用於日常生產。

重點提示 Key Notes

自動化緩解措施：PDA 特別建議，緩解措施應盡可能自動化。例如，當 First Air 原則因物理限制無法被遵循時，自動棄置受影響的產品比依賴人工判斷更可靠。這符合 EU Annex 1 中「減少人為因素」的精神。

APS 納入：所有 qualified intervention 都必須納入 APS 計畫中進行模擬。這意味著 APS 不僅僅是「充填培養基」，還必須包含對所有已批准介入操作的真實模擬。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 情境：假設你的 RABS 填充線在換品時需要更換充填針頭（一種常見的 inherent intervention）。你的資格確認檔案應包含：(1) AVS 影片顯示換針時的氣流模式；(2) 風險評估矩陣記載持續時間上限（例如 3 分鐘）；(3) 與最近鄰無菌表面的距離分析；(4) 操作人員的 SOP 與培訓記錄。只有完成這些文件，此 intervention 才能被列入「approved intervention list」。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果一個 intervention 的 AVS 顯示會短暫破壞 First Air，但該 intervention 在機械上無法避免，PDA 建議的緩解方案是什麼？
  2. 為什麼 PDA 強調「mitigations be automated」？人工緩解有什麼風險？
Q 9.3 Interventions that Disrupt First Air

原文內容 Original Text

Q 9.3. Should interventions that disrupt First Air, as defined in EU Annex 1, be permitted?

Recommendation

The placement of RABS glove positions and the aseptic operation should be designed to avoid the disruption of unidirectional airflow above or in the proximity of exposed sterile product or critical surfaces. Interventions should be designed in a manner that prevents the disruption of First Air to critical surfaces or exposed product. If the intervention is occurring above a critical surface, sterile tools and/or equipment must be utilized for execution of the intervention.

All interventions should be designed following appropriate aseptic techniques as recommended in EU Annex I: Manufacture of Sterile Medicinal Products, FDA Guidance for Industry: Sterile Drug Products Produced by Aseptic Processing-Current Good Manufacturing Practice, or PDA PTC-1. Intervention design must consider equipment limitations and the placement of required equipment (e.g., EM) within the RABS. The use of sterile equipment and tools (e.g., forceps) must be well thought out to not add further risks to intervention execution.

Rationale

The process described above would ensure proper design of aseptic interventions and inclusion in the QRM program through a documented risk assessment to be included in a comprehensive CCS. All interventions shall be designed to meet First Air principles and include proper mitigation if those principles are impacted due to mechanical or physical limitations. The proper design followed by risk analysis and airflow visualization will provide the appropriate understanding of the intervention to approve for use, during routine production, and for execution in a firm's APS program.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

First Air (初始氣流)：EU Annex 1 定義的 First Air 是指直接從 HEPA 濾器出來、尚未接觸任何表面的單向氣流。它是 Grade A 環境中最純淨的空氣。任何介入操作都不應阻斷 First Air 到達暴露產品或關鍵表面的路徑。

設計優先原則 (Design-First Principle)：PDA 的建議核心在於「設計」-- 手套孔位置、操作動線、工具放置都應在設計階段就考量 First Air 的維護。事後補救永遠不如事前設計。

比喻說明 Analogy

First Air 就像瀑布般從上方傾瀉而下的「空氣簾幕」。暴露的無菌產品就在這道簾幕的保護之下。當你把手（透過 RABS 手套）伸入操作時，就像是在瀑布中插入一塊石頭 -- 你會在石頭下方製造出亂流區域。因此，你必須確保你的「石頭」（手）不會出現在需要保護的物品正上方，或者使用已滅菌的工具來延伸你的操作距離。

重點提示 Key Notes

三大法規框架對齊：PDA 特別列出了三個法規文件作為 intervention 設計的依據：EU Annex 1、FDA Guidance、以及 PDA PTC-1。這意味著，無論你的產品目標市場在哪裡，intervention 設計都必須同時滿足這三者的要求。對於 CDMO 而言，這一點至關重要，因為同一條產線可能服務於不同法規市場的客戶。

無菌工具的雙重考量：使用無菌工具（如鑷子）可以避免手套直接接觸關鍵表面，但工具本身的設計、放置和使用也不能增加額外風險。工具越多，操作越複雜，掉落或碰撞的機率也越高。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果 RABS 手套孔的位置正好在充填針上方，你會建議什麼設計改善方案？
  2. 在 intervention 設計審查中，如何平衡「使用更多無菌工具以保護 First Air」與「工具增加操作複雜度」之間的矛盾？
  3. EU Annex 1、FDA Guidance 與 PDA PTC-1 在 First Air 的定義上是否完全一致？如果有差異，CDMO 應如何處理？
Q 9.4 RABS Glove Contact with Critical Surfaces

原文內容 Original Text

Q 9.4. Should contact between restricted access barrier system (RABS) gloves and critical surfaces during setup or operations be permitted?

Recommendation

RABS gloves should not be permitted to contact critical surfaces during setup or during operation.

Portions of equipment would only be considered as a "critical surface" when coming into direct contact with product or components. The handle and exterior surface of the stopper bowl are not "critical surfaces" and may be contacted by RABS or operator gloves during setup.

Aseptic technique should be applied throughout the manufacturing process by trained and qualified operators. (See Question 9.7 for more information on glove installation.) Written procedures are to be established to avoid the risks of RABS gloves contacting direct or indirect surfaces and, if contact occurs, what action(s) are to be taken.

Rationale

While the CCS for RABS gloves should maintain proper aseptic conditions throughout the campaign, there is an inherent risk to the product when touching critical surfaces, as the environment and glove materials are not sterile. Proper controls (e.g., process flow, equipment design) and use of sterile tools should be in place to mitigate the need to touch critical surfaces.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Critical Surface (關鍵表面)：PDA 提供了一個非常務實的定義 -- 只有「直接接觸產品或組件」的設備部位才被視為 critical surface。例如充填針的內壁、瓶塞的接觸面等。而塞栓碗的把手和外表面則不屬於 critical surface，可以被手套接觸。

「禁止接觸」的明確立場：PDA 在這裡的態度非常堅定 -- RABS 手套不應被允許接觸 critical surfaces。理由很清楚：RABS 手套和其所處的環境並非無菌的（不像 Isolator 內部）。

比喻說明 Analogy

這就像餐廳的食品安全規範：服務生可以觸碰盤子的邊緣（non-critical surface），但絕對不能用手觸碰食物本身或食物直接接觸的盤面（critical surface）。如果不小心碰到了，該份餐點就必須被丟棄或重新處理。RABS 手套的邏輯完全相同 -- 你可以操作設備的外部，但不能碰到產品直接接觸的表面。

重點提示 Key Notes

RABS vs. Isolator 的關鍵差異：在 Isolator 中，手套處於 Grade A 環境且經過 VPHP 生物淨化，因此手套表面被視為「可控的」。但 RABS 手套雖然在安裝前已滅菌，但在使用過程中暴露於 Grade B 環境風險。這是 RABS 與 Isolator 在操作層面最根本的差異之一。

必須有書面程序：文件中明確要求建立書面程序 (Written procedures)，涵蓋：(1) 如何避免接觸；(2) 如果不慎接觸了應採取什麼行動。這意味著單純的培訓是不夠的，必須有 SOP。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 請列舉三個你的產線上的 critical surfaces 與三個 non-critical surfaces，並說明你是如何區分的。
  2. 如果操作人員在 intervention 中不慎以 RABS 手套碰觸了充填針外壁，你的 SOP 應規定什麼處置步驟？
Q 9.5 Post Open-Door Intervention Actions

原文內容 Original Text

Q 9.5. What should be performed after open-door interventions?

Recommendation

RABS should be designed and operated with doors closed during aseptic processing; however, the process specificities may require identification, qualification, and approval of interventions performed with the doors open. Interventions performed with open RABS doors (e.g., manual setup) are to be minimized, and mitigation controls must be identified and implemented.

When a RABS door must be opened, those interventions need to be assessed for risk of contamination ingress. These interventions must be part of the approved list and must incorporate additional control measures based on the risk of microbiological contamination that the intervention may produce.

Such additional control measures may include, but are not limited to:

  • Additional disinfection and/or sporicidal disinfection of nonproduct-contact surfaces, including the interior of doors and glove ports exposed or touched during the activity.
    Note: The firm is responsible for documenting and defining a validated agent as part of its CCS.
  • Identification of the appropriate units that are to be manually removed (i.e., discarded) as part of the intervention.
    Note: The firm is responsible for validating all automatic unit removal performed by the filling machine.
  • Collection of sterility samples may be taken, if warranted in the CCS
  • Door access with recorded intervention alarms and an effective means of documenting the following:
    • Start and end time of intervention
    • Description of the qualified intervention
    • Participants
    • Documentation of units removed (i.e., discarded)
    • Documentation of required EM
    Note: The firm is responsible for determining the appropriate risk-based monitoring related to the open-door intervention.
  • Monitoring of operator gloves and additional risk-based locations (e.g., forearms, chest, head, etc.), immediately after completion of the open-door intervention. (See Topic 2 for additional EM recommendations.)

Rationale

Personnel are a significant source of microbiological contamination and, therefore, pose a risk to product sterility. Efforts to separate personnel from sterile products and product-contact surfaces reduce the risk of microbiological contamination. Barrier systems, such as RABS, provide a physical separation between personnel and the external environment and exposed product or product-contact surfaces, which helps prevent microbiological contamination of the sterile product by personnel and the environment.

In the case of open-door interventions, there is no longer a physical separation; therefore, additional control measures are required, as described in this section.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Approved Intervention List (經批准的介入操作清單)：這是 RABS 操作的核心文件之一。每一個可能需要開門的操作都必須事先被識別、評估、資格確認，並列入此清單。任何不在清單上的 open-door intervention 都不應被執行。

五大額外控制措施：

  • 消毒/殺孢子劑處理：針對非產品接觸表面
  • 產品棄置：識別並移除可能受影響的單位
  • 無菌樣品採集：依 CCS 需求判斷
  • 文件記錄：完整的介入操作記錄（時間、描述、參與者、棄置數、EM）
  • 操作人員監控：手套及其他風險部位的即時 EM

比喻說明 Analogy

Open-door intervention 就像是在無塵室中打開了一扇「緊急逃生門」。每次打開這扇門，你都需要執行一套完整的「善後程序」：檢查是否有外物進入（EM 監控）、清潔受影響區域（消毒）、移除可能受損的物品（棄置產品）、記錄事件（文件化），以及確認「大門」已經安全關閉。這不是一個可以省略的流程，就像機場安檢區被突破後，必須清場重新安檢一樣。

重點提示 Key Notes

Intervention Alarm System：PDA 建議 door access 應配備「recorded intervention alarms」。這代表 RABS 門的開閉應該與自動化系統連動，一旦開門就觸發警報並自動記錄。這是減少人為疏失的關鍵設計。

操作人員 EM 監控範圍：不僅是手套，還包括前臂、胸部、頭部等部位。這反映了 EU Annex 1 對 Grade A/B 操作人員 EM 監控的嚴格要求。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 的棄置策略 (Discard Strategy)：對於 CDMO 而言，每次 open-door intervention 的產品棄置量直接影響批次產出率和成本。建議在設備設計階段就與設備供應商討論自動棄置功能（auto-reject），並在確效時驗證其準確性。自動棄置比人工判斷更可靠，也更容易通過稽核審查。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 貴公司的 open-door intervention 後的棄置數量是如何決定的？是基於時間、位置、還是 AVS 結果？
  2. 如果一次 open-door intervention 超過了 qualified maximum time limit，你會採取什麼額外措施？
  3. 為什麼 PDA 說「Collection of sterility samples may be taken, if warranted in the CCS」而不是「must be taken」？這給了企業什麼空間？
Q 9.6 How Should Interventions Be Performed?

原文內容 Original Text

Q 9.6. How should interventions be performed?

Recommendation

Prior to performing an intervention, all product and empty containers are to be cleared, as applicable, then the filling process is stopped. The operator(s) will then don the RABS glove in a slow and deliberate manner, which should immediately be followed by a qualified visual inspection process. The operator(s) then executes the intervention, as described in an approved procedure, following good aseptic practices and the use of a sterilized tool, where appropriate, based upon the intervention.

Upon completion of the intervention, the operator(s) returns the sterile tool, where appropriate, to its designated stand or location within the Grade A RABS. Prior to retracting the hands from the RABS glove, the operator(s) will perform a second qualified visual inspection of the glove. The operator(s) then ensures the glove is correctly placed to minimize stress and ensures the glove does not activate any light curtain, present. The filler can then be reactivated to continue the manufacturing process. When open-door RABS intervention is required, operators should work as a team, with a primary operator performing the task under Grade A environment and a secondary operator assisting the primary operator in the intervention and to ensure proper segregation.

This collaboration between primary and secondary operator(s) during Grade A open-door intervention aims to prevent any contact between the primary operator's gloves and any surfaces exposed to the surrounding environment (i.e., RABS door opening, material transfer). Intrusion of the primary operator and the duration of the intervention into the Grade A RABS should be minimized.

Rationale

Each intervention needs to be performed using a sterile tool to minimize the likelihood of the RABS glove contacting critical equipment and/or damaging the glove. Minimizing the impact to sterile components, equipment, and sterile product, along with the RABS environment, is critical when executing an intervention. Each firm needs to have a robust discard strategy, based on approved airflow visualization, to discard product and open primary packaging components that have potentially been impacted when an intervention is required. It is important to ensure the operator(s) understands and follows good aseptic practices, as they can be a significant source of contamination. The integrity of the RABS gloves is an important part of the comprehensive CCS to minimize hazard ingress; therefore, the RABS gloves need to be inspected prior to and after every use. This process must be proceduralized, and each operator is to be qualified to perform the inspection process. Each intervention needs to be performed using a sterile tool to minimize the likelihood of the RABS glove contacting critical equipment and/or damage the glove.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Intervention 標準流程 (Standard Intervention Workflow)：PDA 描述了一個非常明確的 7 步驟流程：

  1. 清線 (Line Clearance)：移除所有產品和空容器
  2. 停機 (Stop Filler)：停止充填流程
  3. 穿戴手套 + 視覺檢查 (Don Glove + Visual Inspection)：緩慢、刻意地穿戴，立即檢查完整性
  4. 執行介入 (Execute Intervention)：依 SOP，使用無菌工具
  5. 歸位工具 (Return Tool)：放回指定位置
  6. 第二次視覺檢查 (2nd Visual Inspection)：退出手套前再次檢查
  7. 安置手套 + 重啟 (Position Glove + Restart)：確保不觸發光幕

重點提示 Key Notes

Light Curtain (光幕)：這是 RABS 中常見的安全/監控設備，用於偵測手套或物體是否侵入特定區域。操作完成後，手套必須被正確安置，避免誤觸發光幕導致不必要的警報或停機。

雙人操作制度 (Primary + Secondary Operator)：開門介入必須採用團隊合作模式。Primary operator 負責 Grade A 區域內的操作；secondary operator 在外部協助，確保 primary operator 的手套不會接觸暴露於外部環境的表面。這類似於手術室的「術者 + 遞械護理師」的配合模式。

比喻說明 Analogy

Intervention 的執行流程就像外科手術的「刷手上台」程序。你不會直接衝進手術室開始動刀。你必須先完成刷手（穿戴手套 + 檢查）、確認手術區域已清場（清線）、使用滅菌器械操作（無菌工具）、操作完成後逐一確認（第二次檢查），最後安全退出。每一步都有其存在的理由，跳過任何一步都會增加感染風險。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 PDA 要求手套穿戴必須「slow and deliberate」？如果操作人員趕時間快速穿戴，可能會有什麼風險？
  2. PDA 為什麼要求介入前後各做一次手套視覺檢查？如果只在介入後檢查，可能會錯過什麼？
  3. 在你的產線中，primary operator 和 secondary operator 的角色和責任是否有明確的書面定義？
Q 9.7 RABS Glove Installation Methods

原文內容 Original Text

Q 9.7. How and when should restricted access barrier system (RABS) gloves be installed?

Recommendation

RABS gloves are sterilized before installation in the RABS barrier wall (glove port), and subsequently, they must be wrapped and sterilized within an integral bag for protection against contamination through transfer within the Grade B area. Prior to installation, RABS gloves are required to be sterile. Typically, this is accomplished via autoclave or gamma-irradiation. There are multiple ways to install RABS gloves and, while this document outlines three industry approaches, other options may be considered based on the company's equipment and risk assessment.

Note: In all the approaches listed below, there should be no contact of the RABS glove to any Grade A surface with the exception of sterile tools.

Approach 1: RABS Door Closed

  1. RABS door is closed.
  2. Glove port inside is decontaminated by spraying and/or wiping with validated agents (e.g., sporicidals).
  3. Wrapped glove is introduced through the glove port; the glove remains covered.
    Note: The wrapped RABS glove does not leave the UDAF (e.g., within cart) or UDAF zone of protection using a UDAF cart, and it is transferred into the RABS under the UDAF zone of protection.
  4. Upper part of the glove bag is opened using sterile tools (outside of RABS).
  5. RABS glove is connected by the attachment of the o-ring on the outside of the RABS door.
  6. Glove wrapping is aseptically removed inside the RABS.
  7. Glove remains inverted (i.e., turned "inside-out").
  8. Glove wrapping is then taken out of the RABS by using the opening below the RABS doors for oRABS. For cRABS another method must be used.

Approach 1 is detailed in Figure 9.7-1.

(Figure 9.7-1: Approach 1: RABS Door Closed)

(Figure 9.7-2: Example of Approach 1)

Approach 2: RABS Door Open

  1. RABS door is open.
  2. RABS door is positioned and protected inside by an extended, vertical UDAF zone of protection.
  3. Upper part of the glove bag is cut by sterile tools.
  4. Bag gets connected to the glove port.
  5. O-ring is attached on the inside of the RABS door.
  6. Upper part of the RABS glove gets decontaminated by wiping or spraying with sporicidal agents.
  7. RABS door is then closed.
  8. Glove wrapping is aseptically removed inside the RABS.
  9. Glove remains inverted (i.e., turned "inside-out").
  10. Glove wrapping is then taken out of the RABS by using the opening below the RABS doors, for oRABS. For cRABS another method must be used.

Approach 2 is detailed in Figure 9.7-3.

(Figure 9.7-3: Approach 2: RABS Door Open)

Approach 3: RABS Door Closed

  1. Glove port inside is disinfected by spraying and/or wiping with validated agents (e.g., sporicidal agents) based on CCS.
  2. Bag with inverted RABS glove is opened.
  3. Inverted glove is introduced through the glove port.
  4. RABS glove is connected by the attachment of the o-ring on the outside of the RABS door.
  5. Glove remains inverted (i.e., turned "inside-out").

Approach 3 is illustrated in Figure 9.7-4.

(Figure 9.7-4: Approach 3: RABS Door Closed)

By using these three methods, the risk of contamination of the RABS gloves during installation is lowered. This is because the RABS glove:

  1. Was never exposed to the Grade B environment.
  2. Was never in contact with any surfaces within Grade A.

Installing the RABS glove after the last step of open-door interventions required for the setup is recommended.

Rationale

It is common industry practice that sterilized RABS gloves are installed before and/or during the setup of the RABS. Other options for glove installation may be performed; however, careful consideration should be given and a risk assessment should be documented to verify the firms CCS of the RABS gloves with respect to the environment and operator. In order to mitigate contamination by the environment or the operator, the three approaches outlined in this section provide practical options to install RABS gloves.

If RABS gloves are installed following the recommended approaches, any potential contamination of product and critical surfaces with microorganisms should be reduced.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

RABS 手套安裝三法 (Three Approaches)：PDA 提出三種業界通用的手套安裝方法，每種都有特定適用場景：

兩大安全保證：無論使用哪種方法，最終結果都必須確保手套 (1) 從未暴露於 Grade B 環境，(2) 從未接觸 Grade A 內的任何表面。

比喻說明 Analogy

手套安裝就像是在「無菌的氣泡」中進行一場精密的換裝。想像你要在一間無塵室中更換一雙無菌手套，但你的手本身不能碰到手套的外表面，手套也不能碰到房間裡的任何東西。解決方案是：手套被裝在一個密封袋中（像是密封的禮物包裝），你透過手套孔把它送進去，然後用無菌工具打開包裝，再把包裝從另一個出口取出 -- 全程手套都在「保護泡泡」裡。

重點提示 Key Notes

「Inverted」手套的意義：三種方法都提到手套要保持「inverted（反轉/內翻）」狀態。這是一個關鍵的無菌保護策略 -- 手套的無菌外表面（將來接觸 Grade A 環境的面）在安裝過程中是朝內的，從而避免被污染。

安裝時機的建議：PDA 建議在 setup 階段最後一個 open-door intervention 完成後再安裝手套。這樣可以避免剛安裝好的無菌手套在後續的開門操作中被污染。

oRABS vs. cRABS 的差異：Approach 1 和 2 都提到手套包裝可以從 RABS 門下方的開口取出（適用於 oRABS），但 cRABS 需要使用其他方法。這是因為 cRABS 的門在操作期間不會開啟，沒有下方開口可用。

實務應用 Practical Application

滅菌方式的選擇：文件提到手套可以透過高壓滅菌 (autoclave) 或伽馬射線照射 (gamma-irradiation) 進行滅菌。對於 CDMO 而言，gamma-irradiation 的手套通常以即用型 (RTU) 形式購入，簡化了供應鏈管理。而 autoclave 則需要企業自行管理滅菌確效、裝載模式和參數控制。選擇哪種方式應基於產能規模、更換頻率和總擁有成本 (TCO) 來決定。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 比較三種手套安裝方法，哪一種的污染風險最低？哪一種的操作複雜度最高？為什麼？
  2. 為什麼 PDA 建議手套安裝應在 setup 的最後一個 open-door intervention 之後進行？如果先安裝手套再做 setup，會有什麼風險？
  3. 如果你的 cRABS 無法使用 Approach 1 中「門下方開口取出包裝」的方式，你會設計什麼替代方案？
Q 9.8 Disinfection of RABS Gloves During Operations

原文內容 Original Text

Q 9.8. Are restricted access barrier system (RABS) gloves treated with sporicidal agents and/or otherwise disinfected during operations?

Recommendation

The use of disinfection, including sporicidal disinfection, should be defined within a CCS. In general, there is no need to conduct a sporicidal disinfection of RABS glove(s) during aseptic operations.

Note: Disinfection is only required if the RABS gloves come in contact with nonsterilized surfaces.

RABS gloves should be installed, operated, and maintained in a manner in which they will not become contaminated by exposure to the zone of protection outside the RABS (Grade B environment), by contact with personnel during door opening, or by contact with nonsterilized surfaces within the RABS.

This requires that the RABS gloves be inverted (turned "inside out") to the RABS outside when leaving the RABS gloves with the operator hands (See Figure 1.4-1 for visual example of inversion). Leaving the RABS gloves inserted and hanging down inside the RABS should be prevented as they may be contaminated by direct contact with nonsterilized surfaces.

When there are door openings as part of setup or as a qualified intervention during a filling operation, the RABS gloves should also be inverted and should not be directly exposed to the zone of protection outside the RABS (Grade B environment).

RABS glove disinfection or sporicidal disinfection is only required if the RABS glove has come in contact with potentially contaminated surfaces, which are locations below the working level, for example, for interventions where an equipment-part must be fixed. The disinfection or sporicidal disinfection should be performed by wiping; spraying disinfectants inside the Grade A RABS during filling should be prevented.

Rationale

RABS gloves are sterilized before installation and should be installed in a manner that prevents contamination. (See Question 9.7.) Proper aseptic techniques should always be used when working with RABS gloves during closed-door conditions. If the door is not opened, the RABS glove is not exposed to the Grade B environment, and there is no contact with nonsterilized surfaces. There is no requirement for an additional wiping, via disinfection or sporicidal disinfection, during operations. If a contamination risk results as described above (e.g., RABS glove exposure in Grade B, contact with non-sterilized surfaces, etc.) mitigation should follow the recommendations from Questions 9.4 and 9.5.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

手套消毒策略的核心原則：PDA 的立場非常清楚 -- 正常操作下，RABS 手套不需要殺孢子劑消毒。消毒只有在手套接觸了非滅菌表面時才需要。

Inversion（反轉）的關鍵角色：手套不使用時必須反轉（翻到 RABS 外側），使無菌表面朝內受保護。如果讓手套自然下垂懸掛在 RABS 內部，無菌表面可能接觸到設備的非滅菌表面，造成污染。

Wiping vs. Spraying：即使需要消毒，也必須使用擦拭方式，而非噴灑。在 Grade A 環境中噴灑消毒劑會產生液滴和顆粒，反而增加污染風險。

比喻說明 Analogy

手套反轉的原理就像你脫下橡膠手套時自然將其翻面。當你把手從手套中抽出時，手套會自然從手腕處翻轉，原本在外面（接觸東西的面）變成在裡面被包住。RABS 手套也是這個邏輯 -- 不使用時反轉，讓「乾淨面」被保護在裡面，「可能被污染的面」暴露在外。下次要使用時，再翻回來，乾淨面就又朝外了。

重點提示 Key Notes

「Below Working Level」的風險：PDA 特別指出，當 intervention 涉及工作面以下的設備維修時（例如修理充填設備底部的零件），手套接觸非滅菌表面的風險較高。這是因為工作面以下通常不在 First Air 的直接保護範圍內，且可能有潤滑油、灰塵等污染物。

與 Q9.4 和 Q9.5 的交叉引用：如果手套確實發生了污染風險事件，PDA 指引操作人員參照 Q9.4（critical surface 接觸規範）和 Q9.5（open-door intervention 後續措施）的建議來執行緩解措施。這體現了 PDA 文件內部的邏輯一致性。

實務應用 Practical Application

Campaign 期間的手套管理策略：在長時間的 campaign 生產中（可能持續數天），手套管理是一個持續性的挑戰。建議建立一個手套狀態追蹤系統，記錄每副手套的安裝時間、使用次數、是否曾接觸非滅菌表面，以及是否曾進行消毒。這些數據不僅支持 campaign 期間的決策（例如何時更換手套），也是批次放行審查的關鍵輸入。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 PDA 說「spraying disinfectants inside the Grade A RABS during filling should be prevented」？噴灑消毒劑在 Grade A 中會帶來什麼風險？
  2. 如果操作人員忘記將手套反轉就離開，你會如何評估此事件的風險？需要採取什麼行動？
  3. 在你的 CCS 中，手套消毒的觸發條件是什麼？這些條件是否已經過風險評估和確效？

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

參考文獻分類導讀

PtC-12 引用的 20 份參考文獻可以按功能分為以下幾類：

核心法規文件：

  • Ref 1 - EU Annex 1 (2022)：最新版歐盟 GMP 附件一，是 RABS 設計與操作最重要的法規依據
  • Ref 4 - FDA Aseptic Processing Guidance (2004)：美國 FDA 的無菌加工指導，雖然年代較早但仍為有效法規
  • Ref 17 - PIC/S Annex 1 (2018)：PIC/S 版本的 GMP 附件一
  • Ref 10 - 21 CFR 211.65：設備構造的聯邦法規

PDA 技術文件：

  • Ref 2 - TR70：清潔與消毒計畫基礎
  • Ref 3 - PtC (Isolators)：隔離器無菌加工，與 PtC-12 (RABS) 為姊妹文件
  • Ref 7 - PTC-1：無菌加工總論
  • Ref 15 - TR22：無菌製程模擬 (APS)
  • Ref 16 - TR44：品質風險管理 (QRM)

標準與技術參考：

  • Ref 5 - ASME BPE-2022：生物製程設備標準
  • Ref 6 - ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 3：無菌設施設計
  • Ref 12 - ISO 14698-1：生物污染控制
  • Ref 18 - ISO 14644-7：分離裝置標準

重點提示 Key Notes

文獻延伸閱讀建議：如果你正在建立或改善 RABS 操作程序，以下三份文獻是最優先閱讀的：

  • EU Annex 1 (2022) [Ref 1]：理解法規最新要求
  • PDA TR70 [Ref 2]：深入了解清潔與消毒確效
  • PDA TR22 [Ref 15]：設計符合法規的 APS 計畫

特別注意 Ref 14 (Gessler et al., 2011) 關於手套針孔風險的研究 -- 這是理解手套完整性測試重要性的關鍵文獻。

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • 無菌技術一致性 (Q9.1)：不論 closed-door 或 open-door intervention，都必須遵循相同的無菌操作技術。RABS 屏障降低風險，但不消除風險。所有 open-door intervention 需設定 qualified maximum time limit。
  • Intervention 資格確認 (Q9.2)：每個 intervention 須經過風險評估（持續時間、複雜度、接近度、人員暴露），並配備 AVS 文件化記錄。所有 qualified intervention 必須納入 APS 計畫。緩解措施應盡可能自動化。
  • First Air 保護 (Q9.3)：Intervention 設計必須避免中斷暴露產品或關鍵表面上方的 First Air。若因物理限制無法避免，須有文件化的風險評估和緩解措施。設計須同時符合 EU Annex 1、FDA Guidance 和 PDA PTC-1。
  • Critical Surface 接觸限制 (Q9.4)：RABS 手套不得接觸 critical surfaces（直接接觸產品或組件的表面）。必須建立書面程序，定義避免接觸的方法和接觸後的處置措施。使用無菌工具是關鍵緩解策略。
  • Open-Door 後續控制 (Q9.5)：開門介入後需執行五大額外控制措施：消毒、產品棄置、無菌取樣、完整文件記錄（含警報系統）、操作人員 EM 監控。所有 open-door intervention 須列於 approved list。
  • Intervention 執行流程 (Q9.6)：標準化七步驟流程：清線 → 停機 → 穿戴手套 + 視覺檢查 → 執行介入 → 歸位工具 → 第二次視覺檢查 → 安置手套 + 重啟。開門介入須採用 primary + secondary operator 雙人制度。
  • 手套安裝三法 (Q9.7)：Approach 1（閉門，glove port 引入）、Approach 2（開門，UDAF 保護下安裝）、Approach 3（閉門，反轉手套直接引入）。所有方法的共同目標：手套從未暴露於 Grade B，從未接觸 Grade A 表面。建議在 setup 最後一個開門步驟後安裝。
  • 手套消毒策略 (Q9.8)：正常操作下不需要殺孢子劑消毒。消毒僅在手套接觸非滅菌表面時才需要。手套不使用時必須反轉（inverted）。消毒方式為擦拭，Grade A 內禁止噴灑消毒劑。
